106             private String[] getPhoneContacts(Uri uri) {
107                 String[] contact = new String[2];
108                 ContentResolver cr = getContentResolver();
109                 Cursor cursor = cr.query(uri, null, null, null, null);
110                 if (cursor != null) {
111                     cursor.moveToFirst();
112                     int nameFieldColumnIndex = cursor.getColumnIndex(ContactsContract.Contacts.DISPLAY_NAME);
113                     contact[0] = cursor.getString(nameFieldColumnIndex);
114                     String ContactId = cursor.getString(cursor.getColumnIndex(ContactsContract.Contacts._ID));
115                     Cursor phone = cr.query(ContactsContract.CommonDataKinds.Phone.CONTENT_URI, null,
116                             ContactsContract.CommonDataKinds.Phone.CONTACT_ID + "=" + ContactId, null, null);
117                     if (phone != null) {
118                         phone.moveToFirst();
119                         contact[1] = phone.getString(phone.getColumnIndex(ContactsContract.CommonDataKinds.Phone.NUMBER));
120                     }
121                     phone.close();
122                     cursor.close();
123                 } else {
124                     return null;
125                 }
126                 return contact;
127             }

73         	public static String saveBitmap(Bitmap bm) {
74         		File f1 = null;
75         		if (Environment.getExternalStorageState().equals(Environment.MEDIA_MOUNTED)) {
76         			File f = new File(Environment.getExternalStorageDirectory() + "/dz");
77         			// 判断文件夹是否存在
78         			if (!f.exists()) {
79         				// 多级目录创建
80         				f.mkdirs();
81         			}
82         			// 创建存放图片的路径(以时间命名防止被覆盖)
83         			f1 = new File(f, System.currentTimeMillis() + ".jpg");
84         			try {
85         				FileOutputStream out = new FileOutputStream(f1);
86         				bm.compress(Bitmap.CompressFormat.PNG, 90, out);
87         				out.flush();
88         				out.close();
89         			} catch (FileNotFoundException e) {
90         				// TODO Auto-generated catch block
91         				e.printStackTrace();
92         			} catch (IOException e) {
93         				// TODO Auto-generated catch block
94         				e.printStackTrace();
95         			}
96         		}
97         		return f1.getAbsolutePath();
98         	}

25         		if (Environment.getExternalStorageState().equals(Environment.MEDIA_MOUNTED)) {
26         			URL url = new URL(path);
27         			HttpURLConnection conn = (HttpURLConnection) url.openConnection();
28         			conn.setConnectTimeout(5000);
29         			// 获取到文件的大小
30         			pd.setMax(conn.getContentLength());
31         			InputStream is = conn.getInputStream();
32         			File file = new File(Environment.getExternalStorageDirectory(), "updata.apk");
33         			FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(file);
34         			BufferedInputStream bis = new BufferedInputStream(is);

36         			int len;
37         			int total = 0;
38         			while ((len = bis.read(buffer)) != -1) {
39         				fos.write(buffer, 0, len);
40         				total += len;
41         				// 获取当前下载量

43         			}

46         			is.close();
47         			return file;

32         			con.setDoOutput(true);

35         			con.setRequestMethod("POST");

37         			con.setRequestProperty("Connection", "Keep-Alive");

67         			}

69         			ds.close();
70         		} catch (Exception e) {
71         			Log.i("===", "上传失败");
72         			e.printStackTrace();
73         		}finally{
74         			if(br!=null){
75         				try {
76         					br.close();
77         				} catch (IOException e) {
78         					e.printStackTrace();
79         				}

81         		}

528             private File getFile(Bitmap bitmap) {
529         
530                 String sdStatus = Environment.getExternalStorageState();
531                 if (!sdStatus.equals(Environment.MEDIA_MOUNTED)) { // 检测sd是否可用
532         
533                     return null;
534                 }
535                 String name = new DateFormat().format("yyyyMMdd_hhmmss", Calendar.getInstance(Locale.CHINA)) + ".jpg";
536         
537                 FileOutputStream b = null;
538         
539                 if (!PHOTO_DIR.isDirectory()) {
540                     PHOTO_DIR.mkdirs();// 创建文件夹
541                 }
542                 File fileName = new File(PHOTO_DIR, name);
543         
544                 try {
545                     b = new FileOutputStream(fileName);
546                     bitmap.compress(Bitmap.CompressFormat.PNG, 100, b);// 把数据写入文件
547                 } catch (FileNotFoundException e) {
548                     e.printStackTrace();
549                 } finally {
550                     try {
551                         b.flush();
552                         b.close();
553                     } catch (IOException e) {
554                         e.printStackTrace();
555                     }
556                 }
557         
558                 return fileName;
559             }

73         	public static String saveBitmap(Bitmap bm) {
74         		File f1 = null;
75         		if (Environment.getExternalStorageState().equals(Environment.MEDIA_MOUNTED)) {
76         			File f = new File(Environment.getExternalStorageDirectory() + "/dz");
77         			// 判断文件夹是否存在
78         			if (!f.exists()) {
79         				// 多级目录创建
80         				f.mkdirs();
81         			}
82         			// 创建存放图片的路径(以时间命名防止被覆盖)
83         			f1 = new File(f, System.currentTimeMillis() + ".jpg");
84         			try {
85         				FileOutputStream out = new FileOutputStream(f1);
86         				bm.compress(Bitmap.CompressFormat.PNG, 90, out);
87         				out.flush();
88         				out.close();
89         			} catch (FileNotFoundException e) {
90         				// TODO Auto-generated catch block
91         				e.printStackTrace();
92         			} catch (IOException e) {
93         				// TODO Auto-generated catch block
94         				e.printStackTrace();
95         			}
96         		}
97         		return f1.getAbsolutePath();
98         	}

117         	
118         	private  File getFileFrom(String path) throws Exception {
119         		if (Environment.getExternalStorageState().equals(Environment.MEDIA_MOUNTED)) {
120         			URL url = new URL(path);
121         			HttpURLConnection conn = (HttpURLConnection) url.openConnection();
122         			conn.setConnectTimeout(5000);
123         			InputStream is = conn.getInputStream();
124         			File file = new File(Environment.getExternalStorageDirectory(), "updata.apk");
125         			FileOutputStream fos = new FileOutputStream(file);
126         			BufferedInputStream bis = new BufferedInputStream(is);
127         			byte[] buffer = new byte[1024];
128         			int len;
129         			int total = 0;
130         			int num = conn.getContentLength();
131         			while ((len = bis.read(buffer)) != -1) {
132         				fos.write(buffer, 0, len);
133         				total += len;
134         				progressbar.setProgress((total*100)/num);
135         				Message msg = new Message();
136         				msg.what = DOWN_LOAD_NOW;
137         				msg.obj = (total*100)/num;
138         				handler.sendMessage(msg);
139         			}
140         			fos.close();
141         			bis.close();
142         			is.close();
143         			return file;
144         		}else {
145         			return null;
146         		}
147         	}
